 ) There are many ways to recover data from hard disk
 in dinon cloud storage kii vajah external hard discs kaa chalan logon main kam ho gaay he
 But external hard drives are still used
 hard drive ke saath hameshaa se data los kii samasya bani rahati he
 Sometimes the hard disk crashes, sometimes there is a problem in using data due to virus or malware
 virus kii vajah se hard discs ko aapkaa computer detect nahin karata he or is vajah se aapako formet kii jarurat hoti he
 Sometimes data is also deleted by mistake
 aisi sthiti main aapke paas data ricover karne kaa opshan hameshaa rahata he
 This method of recovering data from hard disk will work only when the hard disk is being detected in your computer
 kai baar hardware main problem hone kii vajah se computer main hard diske detect hi nahin karti he aise main ise ricover karnaa bhi mushkil hota he
 Many software or tools will be found on the Internet to recover hard disk

 We show you a way through which you can recover data from external hard disk without any software
 aisa nahin he ki is tareeke se aapkaa 100% data ricover ho hi jaeg
 Because sometimes this method does not work
 lekin aap ise tri kar sakate hai
 Apart from this, some also tell about credible software
 yani agar ye binasoftware vaala trikkam na kare to aap ise software kaa sahaara le sakate hai
 First way (this method is for Windows computer, not Mac) --- Connect the hard drive to your computer via cable
 windows+r press karke CMD tip karen or Command Prompt open karen
 --- Check the drive letter of your external hard drive
 aam taur par ye f yaa g hota he
 Because inbuilt hard drive letters are initialized like C, d and E
 --- ab Command Prompt par ise tip karen ATTRIB -H -R -S / s / d H:*
 * (after ATTRIB, first letter Hago letter of your external hard drive which is here -H) --- The process of file recovery starts as soon as you press enter
 isamen kuch samay lagata he or files ricover ho jate hai
 As we have said earlier, this method does not work due to many technical reasons
 Command Prompt ko aap Run As Administrator se open karen

 inke jariye aap files ricover kar sakate hai

 Your good grasp of geography can be very useful for you
 bhugol main kariyar kii apaar sambhaavnaaen hai
 We are telling you some tips by which you can strengthen the knowledge of your geography topic - 1) You can spend a lot of time on the Internet and gather a lot of information
 jaise ki -vishwa ke vibhinn deshon kii rajdhaniyon ke naam or vibhinn deshon main nadiyon kaa jaal kaise bicha hua he, ye sab internet par sahaj hi uplabdh hai
 Apart from this, good books can also be read by going to the library
 2)vibhinn deshon, mahasaagaron ormausam se sambandhitakitaaben padhein
 3) Do not start with hard books
 apni jaankaree badhaane ke liye pehle bacchon yaa tinegers kii kitaaben padhein
 4) Subscribe to a weekly newspaper or magazine
 saptaah main ek-do artical padhane se aapako bharat kii sabhyataa kii jaankaree hogi
 With this, it will also know which place is in India
 agar kisi jagah baadh zyada aati he to iskaa matlab he ki wo jagah samudr ke kinare sthit he
 5) Visit your local library more and more and read the National Geographic magazine
 isamen bhugol kii gahari jaankaree tasveeron ke saath hoti he
 6) Buy Atlas- Atlas are available at reasonable prices in large bookstores
 agar aapako deshon ke naam yaad karne hai yaa parvat maalaon se aap khud ko parichit karana chaahate hai to maps se shuruyaat kerani chahie
 7) Put the world map on the wall of your house- If your mother tells you that your maternal uncle lives in Mumbai, then immediately go to the map and see where Mumbai is
 agar hawaii main bukamp aayaa he to map main denkhe ki bukamp kaa centre kahaan he
 8) Study the flags of different countries
 9)khud kii pariksha len yaa apane dost ko aapse prashn karne ke liye kahen
 To make it more difficult, ask questions related to the population and capital of the city
 10)vibhinn shaharon, sabhyataaon or aabaadi kii jaankaree local news channels, da wedar channel, sienen, bibisi aadi se mil sakati he
 So watch more and more travel channels, discovery and history channels
 11)deshon or shaharon ke naam par aadhaarit game khelen- maan lijie aapane 'california' kaa naam liya, 'california' khatm hota he a par to aapke dost ko a se kisi jagah kaa naam lenaa hoga 
 You will also enjoy this game and you will also learn a lot
 12)travel karne se bhi aapakinolejbahut badhegi

 from September 2017 to 31 August 2018

 Apart from the fruits in the hilly state of Himachal Pradesh, the medicinal burras are soft-brewed or the plum wine or the savory pickle of the booty- "lungadu", everyone is aware of the taste of Minchi which is the value of local fruits or precious herbs
 Recognizes himalay main milane vaale ''si bakthorn" yaa leh-beri kaa meetha or aushadhiy shitalpeya bhi ab logon ko aakarshith kar rahaa he
 Girish Minocha, an old-fashioned Himalayan product and herb known as grandma's grandmother's home remedies and chronic medicines, has been able to serve the common people
 minocha ne haddiyon kaa dard mitaane ke liye gutti ke naam se pahaado main istemaal kii jane vaali khubaani kii guthli kaa tel bhi bazaar main pahunchaa diya he
 Its effect is considered hot
 pahaado ke beshkeemtee utpaada ko logon tak pahunchane or brand naam se bechney main minocha ko kaaphi mehnat kerani padi
 An electronic engineer by profession and a resident of Shimla, he was determined to do something different
 unhone mushkil halaat kii chunauti sweekaar kii or apane kaarobaar minchi industry kii shuruyaat 1993 main mahaj 10,000 rupye se kii
 Today, after nearly three decades of tireless efforts, Minchi Food Products has a turnover of Rs 15 crore
 tak ho gaya he
 While studying at St
 Edward's School in Shimla and friends at Delhi Engineering College, Minocha was not called by her surname Minocha, but "minchi"
 doston kaa diya yahi pyaar ''minchi" brand ke rup main fail gaya
 Minocha says that his growth is not only due to the processing of flowers and fruits in Himachal, but he always remembers one of the things Grandpa said, "kaka, khan peen da kam ko kita hai, cheesi ohi ki jo jo No one can give his leftovers " maano is baat ko unhone ganth baandh liya or ise minchi ke utpaadon kii gunvattta kii kasuti bana diya
 The challenge to live up to this is always in his mind
 minocha ne ejineering kii degree lene ke baad 1988 main ek nijee company main naukari kerani shuru kar di thi
 But within four months, he started getting bored and left the job
 minocha ko kuch nayaa karnaa tha
 He had collected some money through photography during his college days
 parivaar ke sahyog se shimla ke najadik shoghi main jameen kharidi or nirmaan kaary shuru kar diya
 The first work in 1993 was to make juice
 is kaam ke liye australia se takanic kharidi or america se processing unit laae
 But it was not so easy
 tajurbe kii kami se zeus, jam or kemp kii gunvattta kuch khaas nahin ho pai or 1993-94 main baari nuksaan kaa saamana karnaa padaa
 He also had the idea of starting another business by selling everything for a while
 lekin us aade vakt main patni sonia minocha ne chattan kii tarah unka saath diya or hameshaa utsaah badhaati raheen
 In 1995, when work came back on track, there was encouragement
 sonia ne utpaadan ikai ko puri tarah apni nigaraanee main le liya
 Quality improvement was brought under his supervision
 tab se aaj tak sonia company ke utpaadon kii gunvattta par najar rakhti hai
 In 2003, the cell agency of a wine company that catches Minchi food products to the market started campaigning against them in the market
 usne dukandaaron se kaha ki ve agar minchi ke product bechenge to ham aapako wine nahin denge
 This led to a decrease in sales of Minchi products from the market
 iske baad minocha ne tay kiya ki minchi kii khud kii wine hi shuru kii jaae
 The company launched the wine in 2006 and thus came to the market for the Minci wine with Apple wine
 shuruyaat main mushkilen ain, lekin samay ke saath uski wine ne himachal pradesh sahit desh ke baahar bhi apni jagah banani shuru kar di
 As the business expanded, a second processing unit was started at Sadhupul in Solan district
 bhutan, nepal jaise deshon main bhi minchi kii maang badi or company ne apane product ko un deshon main bhejnaa shuru kiya
 By the way, the popularity of the company's products is that most of the goods are consumed in Himachal Pradesh
 aaj minchi food products ke paas fruit zeus, drink, squash, krashes se lekar jam or wine tak vibhinn prakaar ke utpaada hai
 The company is considered a pioneer in Himachal's fruit wine industry
 yah premium quality kii fruit wine bhi banaati he
 Wines made from fresh and selected fruits are known as Wonder Wine Brand
 minchi kii sadhupul kii unit puri tarah swachaalit he, jahaan do metric ton prati ghante kii utpaadan kshamta vaali mashinari lagaai gai he
 Strict hygiene conditions and traditional techniques are being used in the products
 aajki taarikh main minchi ke paas utpaadon kii vistrut shrenee he
 Minocha credits his success to his friends and family
 lekin apni baat main ve apni patni or dadaji ko nahin bhoolatey
 They have tied the knot of Grandpa's words and they never compromise on the quality of their products
 ve muskaraate hue kehete hai, ''meri safalataa kaa raaj yahi he
 "they point out that market competition also served as an inspiration for them
 ve yaad karte hai, bazaar main jab pratispardhaa badi tabhi ve minchi wine shuru kar paae
 His family was never in this business, but in the lower market of Shimla, there was a ancestral business of ghee-oil
 jamaa-jamaaya yah kaarobaar varshon se chal rahaa tha or ab bhi jari he
 But the desire to innovate transformed the Minocha industry into a Minchi food product
 minocha sanyukt parivaar main rahete hai or ghar ke sabhi log team ke rup main kaam karte hai
 Father Ashwini Minocha and uncle Ashok Minocha still run a shop in Lower Market in Shimla
 betaa surya udai minocha marketing ke saath hi nae idia ke saath product ko aage le jane ke liye prayasarat he
 After establishing his brand, Minocha is now thinking of expanding it
 bharat sarkaar ke saath vistaar ke liye ek samjhauta hua he
 Minocha hopes that as the business spreads, he will be able to create more jobs for the local people
 ve apane utpaadon ko quality ke maamle main antarrashtriya str kaa bananaa chaahate hai
 He has entrusted the responsibility of taking the domestic brand to the people, who is working on a new plan for this
 minocha kehete hai, ''ham apane utpaadon ke jariye daadi-nani ke nuskhe logon tak pahunchane kaa prayaas kar rahe hai
 We have about 150 people working with us
 sabhi sthaneey log hai or ham ise adhik badhaane kii disha main apni koshishen kar rahe hai
 "minocha recalls that there were many occasions in his business when he felt broken and even thought of closing the business
 lekin parivaar ne unhen thame rakhaa or hausala diya
 He was shaken from the inside while launching the Apple wine, but then everything came to a standstill
 puraskaron kaa zikr aate hi minocha ke chehre par ek chaidi muskaraahat khil jaati he
 Minchi never applied for any award
 haa, khaadya mantralay or sisiai kii ore se dilli main yojit teen divasiy sammelan main minchi ne himachal pradesh kaa pratinidhitiv jarur kiya tha
 It seems that Minocha has tied the knot in the matter of Grandpa's point of maintaining quality

 karon or dand ke madhyam se sarkaar ko kitni kamai kii ummid he?ye saare aankade jo charchaa main hai, sarkari nahin hai balki arthshaastriyon or visheshgyon ke hai
 No one can deny that India has a huge parallel economy
 notebandi kaa faisla beshak is kaali arthvyavastha ko baari chot pahunchane ke liye liya gaya tha taaki vah mukhyadhara main aa sake
 However, it was never expected that black money would always be hidden and would not return to the banking system
 ham log shuru se hi is baat ko lekar spasht the ki bade noton ko vittiya tantra main waapas aa janaa chahie
 If it does not, then why would we give the banking system so much time and so many options for the return of notes? If this is not the case, why would we give a period of December 15 for exchange of notes from various routes to pay the government dues from petrol pumps? Therefore, the non-return of large portion of notes in the banking system was neither the agenda nor expected of the government
 hamane vastav main yah mana tha ki paisa, khaskar kaala dhan banking tantra main waapas aa jayega
 This is due to several reasons
 isse 500 or 1,000 ru
 a large portion of the bank's notes come back, which the Reserve Bank had estimated to have been kept out of the flow and stored under their suitcases, cupboards or mattresses
 kahin zyada ahm yah he ki isane ek sthaayee vittiya chhap chodi he
 When the money is returned to the bank, the seal of anonymity is removed from it
 har paise kaa koi na koi maalik hota he
 This causes the game to reverse
 ab tak jo kaala dhan agyaat or anaam tha, vah ab kisi ke naam se he
 Now we know whose he is, where he is from and when
 kaale dhan ke dharak duusare ke bank khate ke peeche apni pahchaan chupa sakate hai, lekin ve jamaa nakadi ke jaise nahin hai or unki pahchaan kii ja sakati he
 He has only a few days left to hide in this hide and seek but the government has ample time, methods and most importantly, willpower to find them
 zyada dilachasp yah he ki aisi nishandehi se bhrashtachar ke or sroton or tareekon kaa pardaafash ho saktaa he
 There are reports in the media that how the officers behind one corrupt person are getting clues of many other misdeeds
 jabt kiye gaye paise kaa istemaal sarkaar kaise karegi?aap is baat ko samajhen ki hamane kisi alpakaaleen laabh ke liye notebandi kaa faisla nahin liya tha balki yah dirghakaalin dhanchaagat badlaav ke makasad se tha
 Our aim was to rid the economy and society of the filth of black money and eliminate the mistrust, fake pressures and other diseases that accompany it
 hamane samanaantar taur par ek kaam yah bhi kiya ki jo log apane taur-tareekon ko badal kar pradhanmantri garib kalyaan jamaa yojana ke madhyam se mukhyadhara main aana chaahate the, unhen ek avasar diya jahaan unhen apni aghoshit aay par baari dand chukaana hoga—30 fisadi kaa kar, kar par 33 fisadi kaa adhibhaar shulk, 10 fisadi kaa atirikt dand or saath hi aghoshit aay ke 25 fisadi kaa byajmukt anivaary jamaa
 The revenue that will come from it will be used for the welfare of the poor, deprived and marginalized people
 is baat kii chintaa jataai ja rahi he ki haal ke ghatnakram maximum gavarnence or minimum government ke aapke vaade ko palat denge
 Critics say the government's role will increase further after demonetisation
 yah kadam iskar ke chhaapon ke raaj kii vaapasi laaegaa or aap iskar adhikariyon, bankeron or baabuon par kahin zyada bharosa kar rahe hai jabaki ve hi sabase zyada bhrasht bhi hai
 What steps will you take to deal with this disease? Earlier, Income Tax officials used to shoot arrows in the dark
 ve apni manmarjee se kisi ko bhi uthaa lete the, kahin bhi kabhi bhi chapa maar dete the or aap jaanate hai ki uskaa nateeja aam taur par kya nikalataa tha
 Today people themselves are coming forward and depositing their money in banks
 iskaa matlab yah he ki vittiya pahchaan sthapit kii ja chuki he, chaahe koi kitna hi isse bachane kii koshish kyon na kare
 This can be easily investigated through technology driven scientific, transparent and objective systems
 aapke sawaal se ulat notebandi vastav main iskar adhikariyon kii manmarjee ko khatm kar degi or bhrashtachar ke khilaaf jang ko ek disha degi
 Taking this further, it will make the tax procedures easier and the relationship between the officer and the tax payer will be smooth
 rajasav vibhaag ek aisi pranali nirmit kar rahaa he jahaan moolyankan kii samoochee prakriya online hogi or karadaata ko adhikari ke samaksh pesh hone kii jarurat nahin rah jaaegi
 We are also using modern technologies and technology more and more, such as big data analysis and data mining
 iske madhyam se padtaal ke liye maamalon kaa chayan vastunishth saakshyon par aadhaarit ho jayega or usamen adhikariyon kii manmarjee nahin chalegi
 The aim is that the honest taxpayer should not be harassed and harmed, while the unscrupulous tax thief can be caught and punished
 iske baad koi adhikari yaa banker agar galati karata he to use dandit kiya jayega
 My government will not tolerate corruption at all
 khabaren aa rahi hai ki nae noton se kaala dhan phir se paidaa ho rahaa he
 What measures are you taking to deal with this? i am glad that you asked this question
 is maamle main bhi ham virodhiyon kii aalochanaon main virodhabhas pate hai
 They argue that black money is not in the form of cash, but in other forms
 baavjood iske vahi log yah kah rahe hai ki nae note kaale dhan main badal rahe hai
 i am happy that now they are accepting that cash has a big hand in black money
 notebandi koi achaanak uthaaya gaya kadam nahin tha
 This is just one step in a series of steps that we have been taking continuously since forming the government, under which black money is flowing and attacking reserves
 iske kuch udaahranon main is sarkaar kaa pehla faisla tha kaale dhan par vishesh kaary bal (esaity) kaa gathan, 2015 main fahrren blike mani kanoon, pan ko anivaary kiya janaa, 2 lakh se upar kii sari nakad kharid par 1 fisadi kaa tisies (strot par liya jane vaala kar), sone kii bikri ko javabdeh banane ke liye aabhushan kaarobaariyon par utpaada shulk tathaa switzraland, morishas or cyprus jaise deshon ke saath soochna vinimay or kar sambandhi tamaam samjhaute
 The time to implement demonetisation was also chosen before the implementation of GST so that the black money reserves can be cleared before its arrival
 bhavishya main kaale dhan ko banane se rokane ke liye hamane pichley do saal main nigaraanee or santulan kaa jo tantra viksit kiya he, jiesti or digital bhugtan uske do nirnaayak tatv honge
 All these steps point towards a transformative regime change where the government is sending a clear message to the people engaged in wrong deeds
 aap digital len-dein or nakadi kii bhoomika ko kam karne ke jabardast pairokaar rahe hai
 Will the extent of digital transactions be able to compensate for the gap created due to lack of cash in the system? What else needs to be done to accelerate the flow of electronic payments? Digital transactions should not be seen as a short-term option during a cash crisis
 meraa yah uddeshy nahin he
 Many people have forgotten that it has been a long time to get this encouragement towards digital
 farvari, 2016 main hi cabinet ne digital vinimay ko protsaahit karne kaa faisla liya tha
 During the last two years, 20 crore people have been given rupay cards under the Pradhan Mantri Jan Dhan Yojana
 digital len-dein se ekaadhik laabh milte hai
 This helps in keeping a book of accounts and knowing its size in the formal economy
 paise ke rakrakhaav main isse suraksha or sahajata aati he, khaskar aam logon or chote kaarobaaron ke liye
 This maintains a financial record that makes it easier to access formal financial systems, including debt
 isse kar anupaalan bhi zyada hota he or yah sunishchit karata he ki beyimaan log apane bhugtan se batch na saken
 That is why i see digital transactions as a tool for cleaning up our economy in the long run
 main aapako ekaadh vaastavik udhaaharan dena chaahunga
 Once informal small businesses start keeping electronic accounts of their cash flows, they will feel comfortable in getting loans
 chota aakaar hone se judi dikkaton se ve paar paa jaaenge
 Similarly, digital payment will protect workers as it will ensure their statutory benefits, which are often not paid in case of cash payments
 isiilie vimudrikaran kai laabhon ko laane vaala ek bada sudhaar he
 The early evidence of this is quite convincing
 logon main digital len-dein kaa istemaal kaaphi teji se badha he
 For example, the use of rupay cards has increased by more than 200 per cent and around 500 per cent at the electronic level and retail level, respectively — both in terms of the number and value of the exchange
 kai logon ko lagata he ki netaa or rajnatik dal bhi kaala dhan paidaa karne ke liye jimmedaar hai
 Taking care of how political corruption can be rooted out, i would like to say one thing first
 bhrashtachar se judi kisi bhi baat ko raajnneeti par laakar patake dene kaa fishan khatarnaak jakadbandi he
 By doing this you create a cover for many others involved in similar acts and they escape
 iskaa matlab yah nahin ki main raajnneeti main bhrashtachar ko jaij maanata hum
 i had said on 8 November that the disease of black money and corruption has penetrated deep into every part of the government, including politics
 raajnneeti se kaale dhan ko khatm karne ke liye jaruri he ki ham nirnaayak tareeke khoj nikaalen
 i am constantly appealing to this
 maine sansad ke pichley satr se pehle is baat par jor diya tha ki vakt kii maang he ki rajnatik chande par ek samgr drushti daalate hue usamen sudhaar laayaa jaae
 i have also consistently raised concerns about how our system of multiple elections not only increases political spending, but also hurts the economy, and as a result, the nation is constantly in the grip of elections, causing the government to stall
 Remains lying hamen chunaav ke is dushchakr ko todgaye ke liye nae tareeke se sochane kii jarurat hogi
 i welcome the Election Commission for the initiative to explore the possibility of holding the Assembly and Lok Sabha elections simultaneously
 vyapak str par dekhen to pichley kuch dinon main hamane paaya he ki vibhinn kshetron se jude logon ke bheetar bhrashtachar ko lekar kitna gussa bharaa hua tha
 The common man has stood firm and determined despite all his personal problems
 paroksh hiton vaale kuch samoohon ne kaale dhan ke khilaaf is jang ko naakaam karne ke liye jaisi tarkiben apanaai hai, log uske khilaaf bhi tanakar khadey rahe
 All of us, especially our leaders and political parties, have to understand and accept this dissatisfaction of the people
 ab baaji palat rahi he
 Those who will not change with it and cling to the old ways will be clean
 apane kaarykaal ko aap aadha paar kar chuke hai
 Are you satisfied with your progress? What is it that you are working on with the vision of creating a country like you? i believe that India is witnessing a historic change today and is on the cusp of realizing its inherent potential as a developed country and global leadership
 is
 ek aisa bharat jahaan kaa kisaan sukhi ho, vyapaaree sampann, har mahila shashakt ho or yuva rojgararat ho
 An India where every family has a house and every family has access to basic amenities like water, electricity and toilets
 ek aisa bharat jo har kism kii gandagi se mukt hokar ekadam svachh ho
 If anyone will evaluate my government's programs and priorities objectively during the last two and a half years, one thing that will emerge is that poor, deprived and marginalized people are present at the center of all these
 hamaari sari pehle inhen ke jivan main badlaav laane ke hisaab se nirmit hai
 At the grassroots level, progress is clearly visible in every dimension and everyone can see it
 mujhe bharosa he ki agar ham ek raashtra ke taur par aisa karne kaa sankalp len to sab kuch hasil kiya ja saktaa he—yah sankalp keval sarkaar kaa na ho balki sava arab bharatiyon kaa ho
